ShotJob[]          @relation(\"ShotJobs\")\n  shotPlanning      ShotPlanning?      @relation(\"ShotPlanning\")\n\n  @@index([sceneId, index])\n  @@map(\"shots\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// Stage4: Semantic Enhancement / Shot Planning / Structure QA\n// ============================================\n\nmodel SemanticEnhancement {\n  id        String   @id @default(uuid())\n  createdAt DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt\n\n  nodeType      String\n  nodeId        String\n  data          Json\n  engineKey     String\n  engineVersion String?\n  confidence    Float?\n\n  @@unique([nodeType, nodeId])\n  @@index([nodeType, nodeId])\n  @@map(\"semantic_enhancements\")\n}\n\nmodel ShotPlanning {\n  id        String   @id @default(uuid())\n  shotId    String   @unique\n  createdAt DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt\n\n  data          Json\n  engineKey     String\n  engineVersion String?\n  confidence    Float?\n\n  shot Shot @relation(\"ShotPlanning\", fields: [shotId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n\n  @@map(\"shot_plannings\")\n}\n\nmodel StructureQualityReport {\n  id ============================================\n// 引擎体系 (EngineHub System)\n// ============================================\n\n// 注意：EngineTask 保留用于向后兼容，新代码应使用 Task 模型\n// EngineTask 主要用于引擎层面的任务记录（scene_parse, shot_plan 等）\nmodel EngineTask {\n  id            String           @id @default(uuid())\n  type          EngineTaskType\n  projectId     String\n  sceneId       String?\n String?\n  // S3-B.2: 引擎版本体系\n  defaultVersion String?\n  versions       EngineVersion[]\n  createdAt      DateTime        @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime        @updatedAt\n\n  @@map(\"engines\")\n}\n\n// S3-B.2: Engine 版本表\nmodel EngineVersion {\n  id            String   @id @default(uuid())\n  engine        Engine   @relation(fields: [engineId], references: [id])\n @updatedAt\n\n  @@unique([engineId, versionName])\n  @@map(\"engine_versions\")\n}\n\n/// Nonce 防重放存储（HMAC 安全）\nmodel NonceStore {\n  id        String    @id @default(uuid())\n  nonce     String\n @@ignore\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 任务与调度体系 (TaskSystem & WorkerPool)\n// ============================================\n\n// Task（平台级任务）\n// 定义：跨 Worker、跨重试、带业务语义的任务\n// 职责：包含任务类型、业务对象关联、重试策略、优先级等平台级元信息\n// 关系：Task → Job（一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job，用于重试）\nmodel Task {\n  id             String     @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  type           TaskType\n  status         TaskStatus @default(PENDING)\n  payload        Json?\n  output         Json? // 任务输出结果，Engine/Worker 执行完成后写入\n  attempts       Int        @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int        @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int        @default(0)\n  error          String?\n  workerId       String? // 实际执行该 Task 的 Worker 节点 ID\n  traceId        String? // Stage13-Final: Pipeline 级 traceId（用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯）\n  createdAt      DateTime   @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime   @updatedAt\n\n  jobs ShotJob[] @relation(\"TaskJobs\")\n\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectTasks\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationTasks\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"TaskWorker\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([status, createdAt])\n}\n\n// WorkerJob（Worker 执行记录）\n// 定义：Worker 维度的一次具体执行记录\n// 职责：记录 Worker 执行任务的过程和结果\n// 关系：WorkerJob 与 Task/Job 是不同层面的概念，WorkerJob 主要用于 Worker 内部调度和计费\nmodel WorkerJob {\n  id            String          @id @default(uuid())\n  type          WorkerJobType\n  payload       Json // { taskData, params, modelInfo }\n  status        WorkerJobStatus @default(pending)\n  workerId      String?\n  retryCount    Int             @default(0)\n  traceId       String\n  jobId         String          @unique // BullMQ jobId\n  engineVersion String?\n  modelVersion  String?\n  createdAt     DateTime        @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime        @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  worker        WorkerNode?    @relation(\"WorkerNodeJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  billingEvents BillingEvent[] @relation(\"BillingEventJob\")\n\n  @@map(\"worker_jobs\")\n}\n\n// Job（Worker 执行单元）\n// 定义：某个 Worker 在某个时间执行某个 Task 的一次尝试\n// 职责：记录单次执行的状态、结果、错误信息等\n// 关系：Job 属于某个 Task（taskId），一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job（用于重试）\n// Studio v0.2: Shot 生成任务模型\n// Studio v0.4: 增强队列化处理能力\n// Studio v0.8: 引入 Task 层，Job 关联 Task\nmodel ShotJob {\n  id             String    @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  episodeId      String\n  sceneId traceId        String? // Stage13: 用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯\n  createdAt      DateTime  @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime  @updatedAt\n\n  shot         Shot         @relation(\"ShotJobs\", fields: [shotId], references: [id])\n  task         Task?        @relation(\"TaskJobs\", fields: [taskId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"WorkerNodeShotJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectShotJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  episode      Episode      @relation(\"EpisodeShotJobs\", fields: [episodeId], references: [id])\n  scene        Scene        @relation(\"SceneShotJobs\", fields: [sceneId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationShotJobs\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n}\n\nmodel WorkerNode {\n  id            String       @id @default(uuid())\n  workerId      String       @unique\n  name          String? // Worker 名称（可选）\n @@map(\"worker_nodes\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 模型宇宙体系 (Model Universe System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel ModelRegistry {\n  id // Relations\n  project      Project            @relation(\"ProjectNovelSources\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  analysisJobs NovelAnalysisJob[] @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\")\n  chapters     NovelChapter[]     @relation(\"NovelSourceChapters\")\n\n  @@index([projectId])\n  @@map(\"novel_sources\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelChapter {\n  id             String   @id @default(uuid())\n  novelSourceId  String\n  orderIndex     Int // 章节顺序（从1开始）\n  title          String // 章节标题\n  rawText        String   @db.Text // 章节原始文本（UTF-8）\n  summary        String?  @db.Text // S1-FIX-A: 引擎对章节的摘要，后续由小说分析引擎生成\n  startParagraph Int? // 起始段落索引（在原始文本中的位置）\n  endParagraph   Int? // 结束段落索引\n  characterCount Int? // 章节字符数\n  createdAt      DateTime @@map(\"scene_draft_status\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelAnalysisJob {\n  id            String               @id @default(uuid())\n  projectId     String\n  novelSourceId String?\n  chapterId     String? //     @relation(\"ProjectNovelAnalysisJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  novelSource NovelSource? @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\", fields: [novelSourceId], engineId      String\n  versionName   String\n  config        Json\n  enabled       Boolean  @default(true)\n  rolloutWeight Int?\n  createdAt     DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime @updatedAt\n\n  @@unique([engineId, versionName])\n  @@map(\"engine_versions\")\n}\n\n/// Nonce 防重放存储（HMAC 安全）\nmodel NonceStore {\n  id        String    @id @default(uuid())\n  nonce     String\n  apiKey    String\n  timestamp BigInt\n  usedAt    DateTime?\n  createdAt DateTime  @default(now())\n\n  @@unique([nonce, apiKey])\n  @@map(\"nonce_store\")\n}\n\n// RBAC 基础表\nmodel Role {\n  id        String           @id @default(uuid())\n  name      String           @unique\n  level     Int\n  createdAt DateTime         @default(now())\n  updatedAt DateTime         @updatedAt\n  members   ProjectMember[]\n  rolePerms RolePermission[]\n\n  @@map(\"roles\")\n}\n\nmodel Permission {\n  id        String           @id @default(uuid())\n  key       String           @unique\n  scope     String // system | project\n  createdAt DateTime         @default(now())\n  updatedAt DateTime         @updatedAt\n  rolePerms RolePermission[]\n\n  @@map(\"permissions\")\n}\n\nmodel RolePermission {\n  id           String   @id @default(uuid())\n  roleId       String\n  permissionId String\n  createdAt    DateTime @default(now())\n\n  role       Role       @relation(fields: [roleId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  permission Permission @relation(fields: [permissionId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n\n  @@unique([roleId, permissionId])\n  @@map(\"role_permissions\")\n}\n\nmodel ProjectMember {\n  id        String   @id @default(uuid())\n  userId    String\n  projectId String\n  roleId    String\n  createdAt DateTime @default(now())\n Cascade)\n\n  @@unique([userId, projectId])\n  @@map(\"project_members\")\n}\n\n// 审计日志（Append-only）\nmodel AuditLogLegacy {\n  id           String   @id @default(uuid())\n  userId       String?\n  orgId        String?\n  action       String\n  resourceType String?\n  resourceId   String?\n  traceId      String\n  ip           String?\n  ua           String?\n  timestamp    DateTime @default(now())\n  details      Json?\n  immutable    Boolean  @default(true)\n\n  @@index([userId])\n  @@index([resourceId])\n  @@index([action])\n  @@index([timestamp])\n  @@map(\"audit_log\")\n  @@ignore\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 任务与调度体系 (TaskSystem & WorkerPool)\n// ============================================\n\n// Task（平台级任务）\n// 定义：跨 Worker、跨重试、带业务语义的任务\n// 职责：包含任务类型、业务对象关联、重试策略、优先级等平台级元信息\n// 关系：Task → Job（一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job，用于重试）\nmodel Task {\n  id             String     @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  type           TaskType\n  status         TaskStatus @default(PENDING)\n  payload        Json?\n  output         Json? // 任务输出结果，Engine/Worker 执行完成后写入\n  attempts       Int        @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int        @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int        @default(0)\n  error          String?\n  workerId       String? // 实际执行该 Task 的 Worker 节点 ID\n  traceId        String? // Stage13-Final: Pipeline 级 traceId（用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯）\n  createdAt      DateTime   @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime   @updatedAt\n\n  jobs ShotJob[] @relation(\"TaskJobs\")\n\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectTasks\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationTasks\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"TaskWorker\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([status, createdAt])\n}\n\n// WorkerJob（Worker 执行记录）\n// 定义：Worker 维度的一次具体执行记录\n// 职责：记录 Worker 执行任务的过程和结果\n// 关系：WorkerJob 与 Task/Job 是不同层面的概念，WorkerJob 主要用于 Worker 内部调度和计费\nmodel WorkerJob {\n  id            String          @id @default(uuid())\n  type          WorkerJobType\n  payload       Json // { taskData, params, modelInfo }\n  status        WorkerJobStatus @default(pending)\n  workerId      String?\n  retryCount    Int             @default(0)\n  traceId       String\n  jobId         String          @unique // BullMQ jobId\n  engineVersion String?\n  modelVersion  String?\n  createdAt     DateTime        @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime        @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  worker        WorkerNode?    @relation(\"WorkerNodeJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  billingEvents BillingEvent[] @relation(\"BillingEventJob\")\n\n  @@map(\"worker_jobs\")\n}\n\n// Job（Worker 执行单元）\n// 定义：某个 Worker 在某个时间执行某个 Task 的一次尝试\n// 职责：记录单次执行的状态、结果、错误信息等\n// 关系：Job 属于某个 Task（taskId），一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job（用于重试）\n// Studio v0.2: Shot 生成任务模型\n// Studio v0.4: 增强队列化处理能力\n// Studio v0.8: 引入 Task 层，Job 关联 Task\nmodel ShotJob {\n  id             String    @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  episodeId      String\n  sceneId        String\n  shotId         String\n  taskId         String?\n  workerId       String?\n  status         JobStatus @default(PENDING)\n  type           JobType\n  priority       Int       @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int       @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int       @default(0)\n  attempts       Int       @default(0)\n  payload        Json?\n  engineConfig   Json?\n  lastError      String?\n  traceId        String? // Stage13: 用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯\n  createdAt      DateTime  @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime  @updatedAt\n\n  shot         Shot         @relation(\"ShotJobs\", fields: [shotId], references: [id])\n  task         Task?        @relation(\"TaskJobs\", fields: [taskId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"WorkerNodeShotJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectShotJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  episode      Episode      @relation(\"EpisodeShotJobs\", fields: [episodeId], references: [id])\n  scene        Scene        @relation(\"SceneShotJobs\", fields: [sceneId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationShotJobs\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n}\n\nmodel WorkerNode {\n  id            String       @id @default(uuid())\n  workerId      String       @unique\n  name          String? // Worker 名称（可选）\n  status        WorkerStatus @default(offline)\n  gpuCount      Int          @default(0)\n  gpuMemory     Int          @default(0)\n  gpuType       String       @default(\"unknown\")\n  tasksRunning  Int          @default(0)\n  temperature   Float?\n  capabilities  Json         @default(\"{}\") // { supportedJobTypes[], supportedModels[], maxBatchSize }\n  lastHeartbeat DateTime     @default(now())\n  createdAt     DateTime     @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime     @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  jobs     WorkerJob[] @relation(\"WorkerNodeJobs\")\n  shotJobs ShotJob[]   @relation(\"WorkerNodeShotJobs\") // Orchestrator Stage2: 关联 ShotJob\n  tasks    Task[]      @relation(\"TaskWorker\") // S1-FIX-A: Task 关联 Worker\n\n  @@index([status])\n  @@map(\"worker_nodes\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 模型宇宙体系 (Model Universe System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel ModelRegistry {\n  id MEMBER\n\n  @@map(\"organization_role\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// Studio: 小说导入体系 (Novel Import System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel NovelSource {\n  id             String   @id @default(uuid())\n  projectId      String\n  novelTitle     String? // 作品名（从文件名或元数据提取）\n  novelAuthor    String? // 作者（从文件内容或元数据提取）\n  rawText        String   @db.Text // 完整原始文本（UTF-8）\n  filePath       String? // 文件存储路径\n  fileName       String? // 原始文件名\n  fileSize       Int? // 文件大小（字节）\n  fileType       String? // 文件类型：txt, docx, epub, md\n  characterCount Int? // 字符数\n  chapterCount   Int? // 章节数\n  metadata       Json? // 额外元数据（如 EPUB 的 metadata，编码信息等）\n  createdAt      DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  project      Project            @relation(\"ProjectNovelSources\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  analysisJobs NovelAnalysisJob[] @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\")\n  chapters     NovelChapter[]     @relation(\"NovelSourceChapters\")\n\n  @@index([projectId])\n  @@map(\"novel_sources\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelChapter {\n  id             String   @id @default(uuid())\n  novelSourceId  String\n  orderIndex     Int // 章节顺序（从1开始）\n  title          String // 章节标题\n  rawText        String   @db.Text // 章节原始文本（UTF-8）\n  summary        String?  @db.Text // S1-FIX-A: 引擎对章节的摘要，后续由小说分析引擎生成\n  startParagraph Int? // 起始段落索引（在原始文本中的位置）\n  endParagraph   Int? // 结束段落索引\n  characterCount Int? // 章节字符数\n  createdAt      DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  novelSource NovelSource  @relation(\"NovelSourceChapters\", fields: [novelSourceId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  sceneDrafts SceneDraft[] @relation(\"ChapterSceneDrafts\")\n  episode     Episode?     @relation(\"ChapterEpisode\") // 关联到 Episode（1章=1集）\n\n  @@unique([novelSourceId, orderIndex])\n  @@index([novelSourceId])\n  @@map(\"novel_chapters\")\n}\n\nmodel SceneDraft {\n  id             String           @id @default(uuid())\n  chapterId      String\n  orderIndex     Int // 场景顺序（从1开始）\n fields: [chapterId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  scene   Scene?       @relation(\"SceneDraftScene\") // 关联到最终 Scene\n\n  @@unique([chapterId, orderIndex])\n  @@index([chapterId])\n @@map(\"scene_draft_status\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelAnalysisJob {\n  id            String               @id @default(uuid())\n  projectId     String\n  novelSourceId String?\n  chapterId     String? // 如果分析单章，指定章节ID\n  jobType       NovelAnalysisJobType @default(ANALYZE_ALL) // 分析类型：全书或单章\n  status        NovelAnalysisStatus  @default(PENDING)\n  errorMessage  String?              @db.Text\n     @relation(\"ProjectNovelAnalysisJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  novelSource NovelSource? @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\", fields: [novelSourceId], NovelAnalysisJobType {\n  ANALYZE_ALL // 分析全书\n  ANALYZE_CHAPTER // 分析单章\n\n  @@map(\"novel_analysis_job_type\")\n}\n\nenum NovelAnalysisStatus {\n  PENDING\n  RUNNING\n  DONE\n  FAILED\n\n  @@map(\"novel_analysis_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// API Key 安全体系 (API Key Security System)\n// ============================================\n\n// API Key 模型（用于机器/Worker/外部服务认证）\n// 支持 HMAC + Nonce + Timestamp 签名机制\nmodel ApiKey {\n  id          String       @id @default(uuid())\n  key         String       @unique // 公钥 ID（对外暴露，例如：ak_xxx）\n  secretHash  String // 密钥哈希（使用 bcrypt 或类似算法，不存明文）\n  name        String? // 可选的 API Key 名称（便于管理）\n  ownerUserId String? // 可选，关联用户\n  ownerOrgId  String? // 可选，关联组织\n  status      ApiKeyStatus @default(ACTIVE) // 状态：ACTIVE / DISABLED\n  lastUsedAt  DateTime? // 最后使用时间\n  expiresAt   DateTime? // 过期时间（可选）\n  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime     @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  ownerUser User?         @relation(\"UserApiKeys\", fields: [ownerUserId], references: [id])\n  ownerOrg  Organization? @relation(\"OrganizationApiKeys\", fields: [ownerOrgId], references: [id])\n  auditLogs AuditLog[]    @relation(\"ApiKeyAuditLogs\") // 审计日志关联\n\n  @@index([key])\n  @@index([status])\n  @@index([ownerUserId])\n  @@index([ownerOrgId])\n  @@map(\"api_keys\")\n}\n\nenum ApiKeyStatus {\n  ACTIVE\n  DISABLED\n\n  @@map(\"api_key_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 审计日志体系 (Audit Log System)\n// ============================================\n\n// 审计日志模型（用于记录关键操作）\n// 支持 JWT 用户和 API Key 两种认证来源\nmodel AuditLog {\n  id           String    @id @default(uuid())\n  userId       String? // JWT 用户 ID，可为空\n  apiKeyId     String? // 对应 ApiKey.id，可为空（HMAC 调用场景）\n  action       String // 动作标识：PROJECT_CREATED / TASK_CREATED / JOB_SUCCEEDED 等\n  resourceType String // 资源类型：project / episode / scene / shot / task / job / worker / auth 等\n  resourceId   String? // 资源主键 ID，可为空\n  ip           String? // 请求 IP\n  userAgent    String?   @db.Text // UA 字符串\n  // V1.1: 记录签名相关字段\n  nonce        String?\n
